[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes past a [0m[1;36m512[0m[39m-byte heap allocation. The overflow originates in `exif_get_sshort`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mcalled via `exif_get_short`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while parsing Apple maker-note data. The issue [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanifests when the fuzzer feeds a crafted `[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m` input, leading to an [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout-of-bounds read and process abort.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer command invokes `exif_from_data_fuzzer` with a single [0m[1;36m512[0m[39m-byte input [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, running it [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m times.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- AddressSanitizer log shows:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - ERROR: heap-buffer-overflow on address `[0m[1;36m0x515000000785[0m[39m` during a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The faulty read occurs in `exif_get_sshort` at `exif-utils.c`, invoked by [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_get_short`.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Call chain:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. exif_get_sshort [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlibexif/exif-utils.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. exif_get_short [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlibexif/exif-utils.[0m[1;92mc:104[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. exif_mnote_data_apple_load [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlibexif/apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.[0m[1;92mc:110[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. exif_data_load_data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlibexif/exif-data.[0m[1;92mc:1010[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. exif_data_new_from_data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlibexif/exif-data.[0m[1;92mc:159[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzzer entrypoint in exif_from_data_fuzzer.[0m[1;92mcc:51[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow address lies [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m bytes beyond a [0m[1;36m512[0m[39m-byte heap block [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x[0m[39m…[0m[1;36m580[0m[39m, [0m        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafter the allocated buffer.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type: heap-based buffer overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout-of-bounds read[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The error triggers while parsing Apple-specific EXIF maker-note segments.[0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39min libexif.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to investigate for a complete understanding:[0m                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - exif-data.c functions `exif_data_load_data` and `exif_data_new_from_data` where[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m208[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview of Root Cause[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Apple maker-note loader in `libexif/apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c` [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder-allocates the per-entry directory size in its initial sanity check [0m[1;39m([0m[39musing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tcount * [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m even though each entry is actually [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m bytes long.  Consequently, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls to `exif_get_short` and friends can read past the end of the buffer, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggering a heap-buffer-overflow.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. High-Level Strategy[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Revise the initial buffer-size check to account for [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m bytes per directory [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add per-entry boundary checks before any field reads.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mirror the robust checks from `exif_data_load_data_entry` in `exif-data.c` for[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboth directory entries and the maker-note data payload.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Correct the Initial Sanity Check[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace the line[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf_size < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m + tcount * [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        with something equivalent to:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          const size_t header_size = ofs + [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m;        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m offset + size of tag count[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+ directory header[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          const size_t entry_size  = [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m;              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m each MakerNote directory [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry is [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m bytes[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          size_t required = header_size + tcount * entry_size;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf_size < required[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                       [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataApple"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Short MakerNote"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              return;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This ensures the buffer holds all directory entries before entering the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloop.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Insert Per-Entry Bounds Checks[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Immediately inside the `for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < tcount; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` loop, compute the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte position:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          size_t pos = ofs + i * entry_size;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        Then verify:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpos + entry_size > buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                       [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataApple"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Directory entry %u out of bounds"[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mi[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              return;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        This prevents any `[0m[1;35mexif_get_short[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + pos, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or similar calls from [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreading past the buffer.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Safeguard Maker-Note Data Payload Reads[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - After computing `dsize = [0m[1;35mexif_format_get_size[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m*components`, if `dsize >[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m`, the code does:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          dofs = d->offset + [0m[1;35mexif_get_long[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + pos + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, d->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        Add:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdofs > buf_size || dsize > buf_size - dofs[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                       [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataApple"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"MakerNote payload out of bounds [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m([0m[32moffset[0m[32m=%zu [0m[32msize[0m[32m=%zu [0m[32mbuf_size[0m[32m=%zu[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m,[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                       dofs, dsize, buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              continue;   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m skip this entry rather than crash[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        This mirrors the style of `exif_data_load_data_entry` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mchecks in lines [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m198[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m207[0m[39m of `exif-data.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. Maintain Existing Logic & Logging[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Use the same `EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA` code and `[0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataApple"[0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtag so existing logging and diagnostics remain consistent.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Ensure that the order of entries and data loading semantics are unaltered [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen buffers are well-formed.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By accounting for [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m bytes per directory entry, we close the gap that allowed [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout-of-bounds reads.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Per-entry checks are cheap and only add a constant-time boundary comparison, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving performance.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Leveraging the established pattern in `exif_data_load_data_entry` ensures [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistency in how libexif guards against malformed inputs.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Legitimate Apple MakerNote data with unusually large `tcount` values might now[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe rejected earlier, but only if the buffer truly lacks the required bytes. Proper [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEXIF data always provides matching directory sizes.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Skipping individual entries whose payload offsets are invalid preserves the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrest of the metadata extraction, falling back gracefully.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Testing[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-run `exif_from_data_fuzzer` against the existing corpus to verify no new [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrashes.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add targeted unit tests for Apple maker-note segments where `tcount` is near [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe buffer limit, ensuring safe early returns.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm that valid EXIF files with Apple maker notes continue to parse [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mequivalent entries.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis strategy fixes the heap-buffer-overflow without touching harness or fuzzing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic, preserves all existing valid functionality, and follows patterns already [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpresent in the codebase’s generic parsing routines.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m[01/02/26 05:44:00][0m[2;36m [0m[34mINFO    [0m Prism Supervisor Routing: TeamStatus.EVALUATE -> TeamStatus.ANALYZE                  ]8;id=875569;file:///home/user/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py\[2m__init__.py[0m]8;;\[2m:[0m]8;id=5378;file:///home/user/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py#160\[2m160[0m]8;;\
